<script>
    // Animation preserved
    document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() {
        const coverageFill = document.querySelector('.coverage-fill');
        const observer = new IntersectionObserver((entries) => {
            entries.forEach(entry => {
                if (entry.isIntersecting) {
                    coverageFill.style.width = '95%';
                }
            });
        }, { threshold: 0.5 });
        if (coverageFill) observer.observe(coverageFill);
    });
</script>

<header class="audit-hero">
    <div class="container">
        <h1>Security Audit Methodology</h1>
        <p>
            This methodology is applied strictly to <strong>authorized scopes</strong>,
            <strong>public repositories</strong>, and <strong>environments explicitly permitted by the client</strong>, following Coordinated Disclosure principles.
            <br><br>
            All research follows <strong>Coordinated Disclosure principles</strong> and focuses on
            CI/CD, supply-chain, and infrastructure-level risks — without exploitation,
            disruption, or access to production systems.
        </p>
    </div>
</header>


<section class="section" style="padding-bottom: 100px;">
    <div class="container">
        <div style="display: grid; grid-template-columns: repeat(auto-fit, minmax(320px, 1fr)); gap: 30px;">
            
            <div class="method-card">
                <span class="phase-badge" style="background: rgba(52, 152, 219, 0.2); color: #3498db;">PHASE 01</span>
                <h3><i class="fas fa-search" style="margin-right: 10px;"></i> Reconnaissance</h3>
                <p style="color: #cbd5e1; margin-bottom: 25px;">Before we run a single script, we map the digital territory. We focus on trust boundaries and hidden entry points.</p>
                <ul style="list-style: none; padding: 0; color: #94a3b8;">
                    <li style="margin-bottom: 12px;"><i class="fas fa-check-circle" style="color: #3498db; margin-right: 8px;"></i> Mapping public-facing assets and DNS records</li>
                    <li style="margin-bottom: 12px;"><i class="fas fa-check-circle" style="color: #3498db; margin-right: 8px;"></i> Deep analysis of GitHub Actions & GitLab CI workflows</li>
                    <li style="margin-bottom: 12px;"><i class="fas fa-check-circle" style="color: #3498db; margin-right: 8px;"></i> Identifying third-party integrations and webhooks</li>
                    <li style="margin-bottom: 12px;"><i class="fas fa-check-circle" style="color: #3498db; margin-right: 8px;"></i> Reviewing baseline IAM policies and access tokens</li>
                </ul>
            </div>

            <div class="method-card">
                <span class="phase-badge" style="background: rgba(74, 222, 128, 0.2); color: #4ade80;">PHASE 02</span>
                <h3><i class="fas fa-robot" style="margin-right: 10px;"></i> Automated Intelligence</h3>
                <p style="color: #cbd5e1; margin-bottom: 25px;">Execution of the <strong>Auditor Core Baseline v1.0</strong>. We deploy our proprietary engine to scan for deep-seated flaws.</p>
                <ul style="list-style: none; padding: 0; color: #94a3b8;">
                    <li style="margin-bottom: 12px;"><i class="fas fa-check-circle" style="color: #4ade80; margin-right: 8px;"></i> Automated secret leak detection in history & logs</li>
                    <li style="margin-bottom: 12px;"><i class="fas fa-check-circle" style="color: #4ade80; margin-right: 8px;"></i> Supply-chain dependency vulnerability analysis</li>
                    <li style="margin-bottom: 12px;"><i class="fas fa-check-circle" style="color: #4ade80; margin-right: 8px;"></i> Container image and Dockerfile security hardening</li>
                    <li style="margin-bottom: 12px;"><i class="fas fa-check-circle" style="color: #4ade80; margin-right: 8px;"></i> Identifying misconfigured S3 buckets and databases</li>
                </ul>
            </div>

            <div class="method-card">
                <span class="phase-badge" style="background: rgba(245, 158, 11, 0.2); color: #f59e0b;">PHASE 03</span>
                <h3><i class="fas fa-user-check" style="margin-right: 10px;"></i> Expert Validation</h3>
                <p style="color: #cbd5e1; margin-bottom: 25px;">The human element. We manually verify every automated finding to ensure zero false positives and real impact.</p>
                <ul style="list-style: none; padding: 0; color: #94a3b8;">
                    <li style="margin-bottom: 12px;"><i class="fas fa-check-circle" style="color: #f59e0b; margin-right: 8px;"></i>  Manual validation of identified logic vulnerabilities under controlled and authorized conditions
</li>
                    <li style="margin-bottom: 12px;"><i class="fas fa-check-circle" style="color: #f59e0b; margin-right: 8px;"></i> Risk prioritization based on real-world impact and threat models</li>
                    <li style="margin-bottom: 12px;"><i class="fas fa-check-circle" style="color: #f59e0b; margin-right: 8px;"></i> Development of tailored remediation code snippets and configuration fixes</li>
                    <li style="margin-bottom: 12px;"><i class="fas fa-check-circle" style="color: #f59e0b; margin-right: 8px;"></i> Final comprehensive report and technical debriefing session</li>
                </ul>
            </div>
            <div style="margin-top:60px; text-align:center; color:#94a3b8;"></div>
        </div>
    </div>
</section>

<!DOCTYPE html>

    <meta name="description" content="Vulnerability Disclosure Policy and Safe Harbor principles for DataWizual Security.">
    
    <link rel="stylesheet" href="css/style.css">
    <link rel="stylesheet" href="https://cdnjs.cloudflare.com/ajax/libs/font-awesome/6.4.0/css/all.min.css">

        </div>

<header class="hero" style="padding: 60px 0; border-bottom: 1px solid rgba(255,255,255,0.05);">
    <div class="container" style="max-width: 900px;">
        <h1 class="hero-title" style="font-size: 2.5rem;">Vulnerability <span class="text-gradient">Disclosure Policy</span></h1>
        <p style="color: var(--gray); margin-top: 10px;">Version 1.2 | Effective Date: January 1, 2026</p>
    </div>
</header>

<main class="container" style="max-width: 900px; padding: 60px 20px; line-height: 1.8;">
    
    <section class="policy-intro" style="margin-bottom: 50px;">
        <p style="font-size: 1.1rem; color: #cbd5e1;">
            This policy governs <strong>good-faith security research</strong> conducted by DataWizual. 
            Our mission is to identify systemic risks in CI/CD workflows and infrastructure while ensuring 
            responsible, non-intrusive coordination with software vendors.
        </p>
    </section>

    

    <div class="policy-grid" style="display: grid; grid-template-columns: repeat(auto-fit, minmax(300px, 1fr)); gap: 30px; margin-bottom: 50px;">
        <div style="background: rgba(34, 197, 94, 0.05); padding: 30px; border-radius: 12px; border: 1px solid rgba(34, 197, 94, 0.2);">
            <h3 style="color: #4ade80; margin-bottom: 15px;"><i class="fas fa-check-circle"></i> In Scope</h3>
            <ul style="list-style: none; padding: 0; color: #cbd5e1; font-size: 0.95rem;">
                <li style="margin-bottom: 10px;">• Publicly accessible code repositories and configurations</li>
                <li style="margin-bottom: 10px;">• CI/CD workflow definitions</li>
                <li style="margin-bottom: 10px;">• Infrastructure-as-Code files (Terraform, CloudFormation, etc.)</li>
                <li style="margin-bottom: 10px;">• Dependency manifests (package.json, requirements.txt, etc.)</li>
            </ul>
        </div>

        <div style="background: rgba(239, 68, 68, 0.05); padding: 30px; border-radius: 12px; border: 1px solid rgba(239, 68, 68, 0.2);">
            <h3 style="color: #f87171; margin-bottom: 15px;"><i class="fas fa-times-circle"></i> Out of Scope</h3>
            <ul style="list-style: none; padding: 0; color: #cbd5e1; font-size: 0.95rem;">
                <li style="margin-bottom: 10px;">• Private infrastructure systems</li>
                <li style="margin-bottom: 10px;">• Live exploitation or interface misuse</li>
                <li style="margin-bottom: 10px;">• Social engineering or phishing</li>
                <li style="margin-bottom: 10px;">• Denial-of-Service testing</li>
            </ul>
        </div>
    </div>
    <h3>Safe Harbor</h3>
    <p>
    This policy is intended to provide Safe Harbor under applicable laws
    for researchers acting in good faith and within the terms described
    herein. DataWizual will not pursue legal action against good-faith
    security research consistent with this policy.
    </p>
<br>
    <h3>Response & Timeline</h3>
    <p>
    DataWizual commits to acknowledge reports within <strong>3–7 business days</strong>.
    Findings will remain confidential until a fix is available or a maximum
    of <strong>90 days</strong> has elapsed, unless mutually agreed otherwise.
    </p>

    <h3 style="color: white; margin-top: 40px; border-left: 4px solid var(--primary); padding-left: 15px;">1. Research Principles</h3>
    <p style="color: var(--gray); margin-bottom: 30px;">
        <strong>Non-Intrusive:</strong> Analysis is limited to public artifacts. <br>
        <strong>No Exploitation:</strong> We never execute payloads against live systems. <br>
        <strong>Privacy-First:</strong> We do not collect or store private data.
    </p>

    <h3 style="color: white; margin-top: 40px; border-left: 4px solid var(--primary); padding-left: 15px;">2. Disclosure Coordination</h3>
    <ol style="color: var(--gray); padding-left: 20px; margin-bottom: 30px;">
        <li style="margin-bottom: 10px;">Private notification via official security channels.</li>
        <li style="margin-bottom: 10px;">Provision of detailed findings and remediation advice.</li>
        <li style="margin-bottom: 10px;">Findings remain confidential for <strong>90 days</strong> or until a fix is released.</li>
    </ol>

    <h3 style="color: white; margin-top: 40px; border-left: 4px solid var(--primary); padding-left: 15px;">3. Safe Harbor</h3>
    <p style="color: var(--gray); margin-bottom: 30px;">
        We consider research conducted under these guidelines to be <strong>authorized</strong>. 
        DataWizual will not initiate legal action against parties who coordinate in good faith.
    </p>

    <div style="background: #1a1c20; padding: 40px; border-radius: 12px; border: 1px solid #333; margin-top: 60px; text-align: center;">
        <h3 style="margin-bottom: 10px;">Security Contact</h3>
        <p style="color: var(--primary); font-weight: bold; font-size: 1.2rem;">eldorzufarov66@gmail.com</p>
        <p style="font-size: 0.9rem; color: var(--gray); margin-top: 10px;">Standard response time: 3–7 business days.</p>
    </div>

</main>

<footer class="footer">
    <div class="container" style="text-align: center;">
        <p style="color: var(--gray); font-size: 0.9rem;">
            &copy; 2026 DataWizual Security. All research conducted for a safer supply chain.
        </p>
    </div>
</footer>

    <title>Sentinel | Deterministic Security Gate for CI/CD | DataWizual</title>
    <meta name="description" content="Stop threats before they emerge. Sentinel enforces security policies at the commit level, creating an impenetrable development perimeter.">
    
    <link rel="stylesheet" href="css/style.css">
    <link rel="stylesheet" href="https://cdnjs.cloudflare.com/ajax/libs/font-awesome/6.4.0/css/all.min.css">

    <style>
        /* Sentinel-specific animations */

<section class="section" style="padding: 100px 0; background: rgba(15, 23, 42, 0.7);">
    <div class="container">
        <h2 style="text-align: center; margin-bottom: 20px; font-size: 2.8rem;">
            Deterministic by <span class="text-gradient">Design</span>
        </h2>
        <p style="text-align: center; color: var(--gray); margin-bottom: 60px; font-size: 1.1rem; max-width: 800px; margin-left: auto; margin-right: auto;">
            Unlike scanners that provide risk opinions, Sentinel delivers authoritative decisions. 
            Every execution results in exactly one of two states.
        </p>
        
        <div style="display: grid; grid-template-columns: repeat(auto-fit, minmax(300px, 1fr)); gap: 30px; margin-bottom: 60px;">
            
            <div class="rule-card" style="text-align: center;">
                <div style="width: 70px; height: 70px; background: rgba(74, 222, 128, 0.1); border-radius: 50%; display: flex; align-items: center; justify-content: center; margin: 0 auto 25px;">
                    <i class="fas fa-check-circle" style="font-size: 2rem; color: #4ade80;"></i>
                </div>
                <h3 style="margin-bottom: 15px; color: white;">ALLOW (0)</h3>
                <p style="color: var(--gray); line-height: 1.6;">
                    Zero violations detected. Code meets all security policies. 
                    Pipeline proceeds without interruption.
                </p>
                <div style="margin-top: 20px;">
                    <span class="decision-badge decision-allow">Pipeline Proceeds</span>
                </div>
            </div>
            
            <div class="rule-card block-strike" style="text-align: center;">
                <div style="width: 70px; height: 70px; background: rgba(239, 68, 68, 0.1); border-radius: 50%; display: flex; align-items: center; justify-content: center; margin: 0 auto 25px;">
                    <i class="fas fa-ban" style="font-size: 2rem; color: #f87171;"></i>
                </div>
                <h3 style="margin-bottom: 15px; color: white;">BLOCK (1)</h3>
                <p style="color: var(--gray); line-height: 1.6;">
                    Unapproved critical violations detected. 
                    Pipeline terminates immediately. Code cannot proceed.
                </p>
                <div style="margin-top: 20px;">
                    <span class="decision-badge decision-block">Pipeline Terminated</span>
                </div>
            </div>
            
            <div class="rule-card" style="text-align: center;">
                <div style="width: 70px; height: 70px; background: rgba(245, 158, 11, 0.1); border-radius: 50%; display: flex; align-items: center; justify-content: center; margin: 0 auto 25px;">
                    <i class="fas fa-exclamation-triangle" style="font-size: 2rem; color: #f59e0b;"></i>
                </div>
                <h3 style="margin-bottom: 15px; color: white;">WARN (Audited)</h3>
                <p style="color: var(--gray); line-height: 1.6;">
                    Overridden violations with formal justification. 
                    Pipeline proceeds with explicit audit trail.
                </p>
                <div style="margin-top: 20px;">
                    <span class="decision-badge decision-warn">Audited Exception</span>
                </div>
            </div>
            
        </div>
        
        <div style="background: rgba(26, 28, 32, 0.8); border-radius: 16px; padding: 40px; border: 1px solid rgba(255,255,255,0.05);">
            <h3 style="color: white; margin-bottom: 20px; text-align: center;">
                <i class="fas fa-clipboard-check"></i> Audit-First Exception Model
            </h3>
            <p style="color: var(--gray); text-align: center; max-width: 800px; margin: 0 auto 30px;">
                Sentinel uses an auditable exception model. Violations cannot be silently ignored; 
                they must be formally justified in <code>sentinel.yaml</code>.
            </p>
            
            <div style="background: #1a1c20; border-radius: 8px; padding: 25px; font-family: 'Courier New', monospace; font-size: 14px; color: #eee; max-width: 600px; margin: 0 auto;">
                <div style="color: #94a3b8; margin-bottom: 15px;"># sentinel.yaml - Policy Overrides</div>
                <div style="color: #f59e0b;">overrides:</div>
                <div style="margin-left: 20px;">
                    <div style="color: #94a3b8;">- <span style="color: #4ade80;">rule_id</span>: "SUPPLY-001"</div>
                    <div style="color: #94a3b8; margin-left: 20px;"><span style="color: #4ade80;">justification</span>: "Legacy base image required for test-suite compatibility"</div>
                    <div style="margin-top: 10px; color: #94a3b8;">- <span style="color: #4ade80;">rule_id</span>: "SEC-001"</div>
                    <div style="color: #94a3b8; margin-left: 20px;"><span style="color: #4ade80;">justification</span>: "Verified public mock token for internal tests"</div>
                </div>
            </div>
        </div>
    </div>
</section>

<section class="section" style="padding: 100px 0; background: rgba(15, 23, 42, 0.7);">
    <div class="container">
        <h2 style="text-align: center; margin-bottom: 20px; font-size: 2.8rem;">
            <span class="text-gradient">Zero-Leakage</span> & Offline Guarantee
        </h2>
        <p style="text-align: center; color: var(--gray); margin-bottom: 60px; font-size: 1.1rem; max-width: 800px; margin-left: auto; margin-right: auto;">
            Sentinel forbids all network access at runtime by design. Safe for air-gapped environments.
        </p>
        
        <div style="display: grid; grid-template-columns: repeat(auto-fit, minmax(300px, 1fr)); gap: 30px;">
            
            <div class="zero-leakage">
                <div style="width: 80px; height: 80px; background: rgba(239, 68, 68, 0.1); border-radius: 50%; display: flex; align-items: center; justify-content: center; margin: 0 auto 25px;">
                    <i class="fas fa-ban" style="font-size: 2.5rem; color: #f87171;"></i>
                </div>
                <h3 style="margin-bottom: 15px; color: white;">No Telemetry</h3>
                <p style="color: var(--gray); line-height: 1.6;">
                    No usage data is ever collected. Sentinel operates without phoning home.
                </p>
            </div>
            
            <div class="zero-leakage">
                <div style="width: 80px; height: 80px; background: rgba(74, 222, 128, 0.1); border-radius: 50%; display: flex; align-items: center; justify-content: center; margin: 0 auto 25px;">
                    <i class="fas fa-wifi-slash" style="font-size: 2.5rem; color: #4ade80;"></i>
                </div>
                <h3 style="margin-bottom: 15px; color: white;">Air-Gap Ready</h3>
                <p style="color: var(--gray); line-height: 1.6;">
                    Operates without internet access. Safe for highly restricted internal environments.
                </p>
            </div>
            
            <div class="zero-leakage">
                <div style="width: 80px; height: 80px; background: rgba(52, 152, 219, 0.1); border-radius: 50%; display: flex; align-items: center; justify-content: center; margin: 0 auto 25px;">
                    <i class="fas fa-download" style="font-size: 2.5rem; color: var(--primary);"></i>
                </div>
                <h3 style="margin-bottom: 15px; color: white;">Immutable Logic</h3>
                <p style="color: var(--gray); line-height: 1.6;">
                    Never self-updates or pulls remote rules at runtime. Security logic is guaranteed.
                </p>
            </div>

<script>
    // Gate interaction demo
    function toggleGate() {
        const gate = document.getElementById('gateDemo');
        const status = document.getElementById('gateStatus');
        const message = document.getElementById('gateMessage');
        const decisionStage = document.getElementById('decisionStage');
        const decisionBadge = decisionStage.querySelector('.decision-badge');
        
        if (gate.classList.contains('gate-open')) {
            // Reset to ALLOW
            gate.classList.remove('gate-open');
            status.textContent = 'ACTIVE';
            status.style.color = '#4ade80';
            message.innerHTML = '✓ Security policy satisfied';
            message.style.color = '#4ade80';
            
            decisionStage.classList.remove('blocked');
            decisionStage.classList.add('sentinel-active');
            decisionBadge.className = 'decision-badge decision-allow';
            decisionBadge.textContent = 'ALLOW';
        } else {
            // Simulate BLOCK
            gate.classList.add('gate-open');
            status.textContent = 'BLOCKED';
            status.style.color = '#f87171';
            message.innerHTML = '✗ Policy violation detected: SUPPLY-001';
            message.style.color = '#f87171';
            
            decisionStage.classList.remove('sentinel-active');
            decisionStage.classList.add('blocked');
            decisionBadge.className = 'decision-badge decision-block';
            decisionBadge.textContent = 'BLOCK';
        }
    }
    
    function resetGate() {
        const gate = document.getElementById('gateDemo');
        const status = document.getElementById('gateStatus');
        const message = document.getElementById('gateMessage');
        const decisionStage = document.getElementById('decisionStage');
        const decisionBadge = decisionStage.querySelector('.decision-badge');
        
        gate.classList.remove('gate-open');
        status.textContent = 'ACTIVE';
        status.style.color = '#4ade80';
        message.innerHTML = '✓ Security policy satisfied';
        message.style.color = '#4ade80';
        
        decisionStage.classList.remove('blocked');
        decisionStage.classList.add('sentinel-active');
        decisionBadge.className = 'decision-badge decision-allow';
        decisionBadge.textContent = 'ALLOW';
    }
    
    // Initialize gate
    document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() {
        const decisionStage = document.getElementById('decisionStage');
        decisionStage.classList.add('sentinel-active');
    }); 
</script>

</body>
</html>

    // Animation preserved
    document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() {
        const coverageFill = document.querySelector('.coverage-fill');
        const observer = new IntersectionObserver((entries) => {
            entries.forEach(entry => {
                if (entry.isIntersecting) {
                    coverageFill.style.width = '95%';
                }
            });
        }, { threshold: 0.5 });
        if (coverageFill) observer.observe(coverageFill);
    });
</script>

        <p>
            This methodology is applied strictly to <strong>authorized scopes</strong>,
            <strong>public repositories</strong>, and <strong>environments explicitly permitted by the client</strong>, following Coordinated Disclosure principles.
            <br><br>
            All research follows <strong>Coordinated Disclosure principles</strong> and focuses on
            CI/CD, supply-chain, and infrastructure-level risks — without exploitation,

<section class="section" style="padding-bottom: 100px;">
    <div class="container">
        <div style="display: grid; grid-template-columns: repeat(auto-fit, minmax(320px, 1fr)); gap: 30px;">
            
            <div class="method-card">
                <span class="phase-badge" style="background: rgba(52, 152, 219, 0.2); color: #3498db;">PHASE 01</span>
                <h3><i class="fas fa-search" style="margin-right: 10px;"></i> Reconnaissance</h3>
                <p style="color: #cbd5e1; margin-bottom: 25px;">Before we run a single script, we map the digital territory. We focus on trust boundaries and hidden entry points.</p>
                <ul style="list-style: none; padding: 0; color: #94a3b8;">
                    <li style="margin-bottom: 12px;"><i class="fas fa-check-circle" style="color: #3498db; margin-right: 8px;"></i> Mapping public-facing assets and DNS records</li>
                    <li style="margin-bottom: 12px;"><i class="fas fa-check-circle" style="color: #3498db; margin-right: 8px;"></i> Deep analysis of GitHub Actions & GitLab CI workflows</li>
                    <li style="margin-bottom: 12px;"><i class="fas fa-check-circle" style="color: #3498db; margin-right: 8px;"></i> Identifying third-party integrations and webhooks</li>
                    <li style="margin-bottom: 12px;"><i class="fas fa-check-circle" style="color: #3498db; margin-right: 8px;"></i> Reviewing baseline IAM policies and access tokens</li>
                </ul>
            </div>

            <div class="method-card">
                <span class="phase-badge" style="background: rgba(74, 222, 128, 0.2); color: #4ade80;">PHASE 02</span>
                <h3><i class="fas fa-robot" style="margin-right: 10px;"></i> Automated Intelligence</h3>
                <p style="color: #cbd5e1; margin-bottom: 25px;">Execution of the <strong>Auditor Core Baseline v1.0</strong>. We deploy our proprietary engine to scan for deep-seated flaws.</p>
                <ul style="list-style: none; padding: 0; color: #94a3b8;">
                    <li style="margin-bottom: 12px;"><i class="fas fa-check-circle" style="color: #4ade80; margin-right: 8px;"></i> Automated secret leak detection in history & logs</li>
                    <li style="margin-bottom: 12px;"><i class="fas fa-check-circle" style="color: #4ade80; margin-right: 8px;"></i> Supply-chain dependency vulnerability analysis</li>
                    <li style="margin-bottom: 12px;"><i class="fas fa-check-circle" style="color: #4ade80; margin-right: 8px;"></i> Container image and Dockerfile security hardening</li>
                    <li style="margin-bottom: 12px;"><i class="fas fa-check-circle" style="color: #4ade80; margin-right: 8px;"></i> Identifying misconfigured S3 buckets and databases</li>
                </ul>
            </div>

            <div class="method-card">
                <span class="phase-badge" style="background: rgba(245, 158, 11, 0.2); color: #f59e0b;">PHASE 03</span>
                <h3><i class="fas fa-user-check" style="margin-right: 10px;"></i> Expert Validation</h3>
                <p style="color: #cbd5e1; margin-bottom: 25px;">The human element. We manually verify every automated finding to ensure zero false positives and real impact.</p>
                <ul style="list-style: none; padding: 0; color: #94a3b8;">
                    <li style="margin-bottom: 12px;"><i class="fas fa-check-circle" style="color: #f59e0b; margin-right: 8px;"></i>  Manual validation of identified logic vulnerabilities under controlled and authorized conditions
</li>
                    <li style="margin-bottom: 12px;"><i class="fas fa-check-circle" style="color: #f59e0b; margin-right: 8px;"></i> Risk prioritization based on real-world impact and threat models</li>
                    <li style="margin-bottom: 12px;"><i class="fas fa-check-circle" style="color: #f59e0b; margin-right: 8px;"></i> Development of tailored remediation code snippets and configuration fixes</li>
                    <li style="margin-bottom: 12px;"><i class="fas fa-check-circle" style="color: #f59e0b; margin-right: 8px;"></i> Final comprehensive report and technical debriefing session</li>
                </ul>

                            <span class="rule-id">ci.privileged_container</span>
                            Container running with privileged access in CI pipeline definition.
                        </td>
                        <td style="color: #ea580c; font-weight: 700;">HIGH</td>
                        <td>CWE-269</td>
                        <td class="path-text">.github/workflows/deploy-main.yml:24</td>
                    </tr>

                            <span class="rule-id">infra.unencrypted_transport</span>
                            Internal microservice communication detected over plaintext HTTP.
                        </td>

                        <td>CWE-319</td>

                    </tr>

            </table>

<header class="hero" style="padding: 60px 0; border-bottom: 1px solid rgba(255,255,255,0.05);">
    <div class="container" style="max-width: 900px;">
        <h1 class="hero-title" style="font-size: 2.5rem;">Vulnerability <span class="text-gradient">Disclosure Policy</span></h1>
        <p style="color: var(--gray); margin-top: 10px;">Version 1.2 | Effective Date: January 1, 2026</p>
    </div>
</header>

<main class="container" style="max-width: 900px; padding: 60px 20px; line-height: 1.8;">
    
    <section class="policy-intro" style="margin-bottom: 50px;">
        <p style="font-size: 1.1rem; color: #cbd5e1;">
            This policy governs <strong>good-faith security research</strong> conducted by DataWizual. 
            Our mission is to identify systemic risks in CI/CD workflows and infrastructure while ensuring 
            responsible, non-intrusive coordination with software vendors.
        </p>
    </section>

    

    <div class="policy-grid" style="display: grid; grid-template-columns: repeat(auto-fit, minmax(300px, 1fr)); gap: 30px; margin-bottom: 50px;">
        <div style="background: rgba(34, 197, 94, 0.05); padding: 30px; border-radius: 12px; border: 1px solid rgba(34, 197, 94, 0.2);">
            <h3 style="color: #4ade80; margin-bottom: 15px;"><i class="fas fa-check-circle"></i> In Scope</h3>
            <ul style="list-style: none; padding: 0; color: #cbd5e1; font-size: 0.95rem;">
                <li style="margin-bottom: 10px;">• Publicly accessible code repositories and configurations</li>
                <li style="margin-bottom: 10px;">• CI/CD workflow definitions</li>
                <li style="margin-bottom: 10px;">• Infrastructure-as-Code files (Terraform, CloudFormation, etc.)</li>
                <li style="margin-bottom: 10px;">• Dependency manifests (package.json, requirements.txt, etc.)</li>
            </ul>
        </div>

        <div style="background: rgba(239, 68, 68, 0.05); padding: 30px; border-radius: 12px; border: 1px solid rgba(239, 68, 68, 0.2);">
            <h3 style="color: #f87171; margin-bottom: 15px;"><i class="fas fa-times-circle"></i> Out of Scope</h3>
            <ul style="list-style: none; padding: 0; color: #cbd5e1; font-size: 0.95rem;">
                <li style="margin-bottom: 10px;">• Private infrastructure systems</li>
                <li style="margin-bottom: 10px;">• Live exploitation or interface misuse</li>
                <li style="margin-bottom: 10px;">• Social engineering or phishing</li>
                <li style="margin-bottom: 10px;">• Denial-of-Service testing</li>
            </ul>
        </div>
    </div>
    <h3>Safe Harbor</h3>
    <p>
    This policy is intended to provide Safe Harbor under applicable laws
    for researchers acting in good faith and within the terms described
    herein. DataWizual will not pursue legal action against good-faith
    security research consistent with this policy.
    </p>
<br>
    <h3>Response & Timeline</h3>
    <p>
    DataWizual commits to acknowledge reports within <strong>3–7 business days</strong>.
    Findings will remain confidential until a fix is available or a maximum
    of <strong>90 days</strong> has elapsed, unless mutually agreed otherwise.
    </p>

    <h3 style="color: white; margin-top: 40px; border-left: 4px solid var(--primary); padding-left: 15px;">1. Research Principles</h3>
    <p style="color: var(--gray); margin-bottom: 30px;">
        <strong>Non-Intrusive:</strong> Analysis is limited to public artifacts. <br>
        <strong>No Exploitation:</strong> We never execute payloads against live systems. <br>
        <strong>Privacy-First:</strong> We do not collect or store private data.
    </p>

    <h3 style="color: white; margin-top: 40px; border-left: 4px solid var(--primary); padding-left: 15px;">2. Disclosure Coordination</h3>
    <ol style="color: var(--gray); padding-left: 20px; margin-bottom: 30px;">
        <li style="margin-bottom: 10px;">Private notification via official security channels.</li>
        <li style="margin-bottom: 10px;">Provision of detailed findings and remediation advice.</li>
        <li style="margin-bottom: 10px;">Findings remain confidential for <strong>90 days</strong> or until a fix is released.</li>
    </ol>

    <h3 style="color: white; margin-top: 40px; border-left: 4px solid var(--primary); padding-left: 15px;">3. Safe Harbor</h3>
    <p style="color: var(--gray); margin-bottom: 30px;">
        We consider research conducted under these guidelines to be <strong>authorized</strong>. 
        DataWizual will not initiate legal action against parties who coordinate in good faith.
    </p>

    <div style="background: #1a1c20; padding: 40px; border-radius: 12px; border: 1px solid #333; margin-top: 60px; text-align: center;">
        <h3 style="margin-bottom: 10px;">Security Contact</h3>
        <p style="color: var(--primary); font-weight: bold; font-size: 1.2rem;">eldorzufarov66@gmail.com</p>
        <p style="font-size: 0.9rem; color: var(--gray); margin-top: 10px;">Standard response time: 3–7 business days.</p>
    </div>

</main>

<footer class="footer">
    <div class="container" style="text-align: center;">
        <p style="color: var(--gray); font-size: 0.9rem;">
            &copy; 2026 DataWizual Security. All research conducted for a safer supply chain.
        </p>
    </div>
</footer>

<section id="how-it-works" class="section" style="padding: 100px 0; background: var(--dark);">
    <div class="container">
        <h2 style="text-align: center; margin-bottom: 20px; font-size: 2.8rem;">
            How <span class="text-gradient">Sentinel Works</span>

<script>
    // Gate interaction demo
    function toggleGate() {
        const gate = document.getElementById('gateDemo');
        const status = document.getElementById('gateStatus');
        const message = document.getElementById('gateMessage');
        const decisionStage = document.getElementById('decisionStage');
        const decisionBadge = decisionStage.querySelector('.decision-badge');
        
        if (gate.classList.contains('gate-open')) {
            // Reset to ALLOW
            gate.classList.remove('gate-open');
            status.textContent = 'ACTIVE';
            status.style.color = '#4ade80';
            message.innerHTML = '✓ Security policy satisfied';
            message.style.color = '#4ade80';
            
            decisionStage.classList.remove('blocked');
            decisionStage.classList.add('sentinel-active');
            decisionBadge.className = 'decision-badge decision-allow';
            decisionBadge.textContent = 'ALLOW';
        } else {
            // Simulate BLOCK
            gate.classList.add('gate-open');
            status.textContent = 'BLOCKED';
            status.style.color = '#f87171';
            message.innerHTML = '✗ Policy violation detected: SUPPLY-001';
            message.style.color = '#f87171';
            
            decisionStage.classList.remove('sentinel-active');
            decisionStage.classList.add('blocked');
            decisionBadge.className = 'decision-badge decision-block';
            decisionBadge.textContent = 'BLOCK';
        }
    }
    
    function resetGate() {
        const gate = document.getElementById('gateDemo');
        const status = document.getElementById('gateStatus');
        const message = document.getElementById('gateMessage');
        const decisionStage = document.getElementById('decisionStage');
        const decisionBadge = decisionStage.querySelector('.decision-badge');
        
        gate.classList.remove('gate-open');
        status.textContent = 'ACTIVE';
        status.style.color = '#4ade80';
        message.innerHTML = '✓ Security policy satisfied';
        message.style.color = '#4ade80';
        
        decisionStage.classList.remove('blocked');
        decisionStage.classList.add('sentinel-active');
        decisionBadge.className = 'decision-badge decision-allow';
        decisionBadge.textContent = 'ALLOW';
    }
    
    // Initialize gate
    document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() {
        const decisionStage = document.getElementById('decisionStage');
        decisionStage.classList.add('sentinel-active');
    }); 
</script>

</body>

FILE: js/script.js

// Main script for DataWizual Security
console.log('DataWizual Security Engine Loaded');

// Smooth scrolling for anchor links
document.querySelectorAll('a[href^="#"]').forEach(anchor => {
    anchor.addEventListener('click', function(e) {
        const href = this.getAttribute('href');
        if (href === '#') return;
        
        e.preventDefault();
        const targetElement = document.querySelector(href);
        if (targetElement) {
            window.scrollTo({
                top: targetElement.offsetTop - 80,
                behavior: 'smooth'
            });
        }
    });
});

// Logic for Access Request
function handleAccessRequest() {
    window.location.href = "mailto:eldorzufarov66@gmail.com?subject=Access%20Request:%20Auditor%20Core%20Pro";
}

// Fade-in effect on scroll
const observerOptions = { threshold: 0.1 };
const observer = new IntersectionObserver((entries) => {
    entries.forEach(entry => {
        if (entry.isIntersecting) {
            entry.target.style.opacity = "1";
            entry.target.style.transform = "translateY(0)";
        }
    });
}, observerOptions);

document.querySelectorAll('.section').forEach(section => {
    section.style.opacity = "0";
    section.style.transform = "translateY(20px)";
    section.style.transition = "all 0.8s ease-out";
    observer.observe(section);
});
